    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_48;

    u_xlat16_7 = (-u_xlat16_6);

    u_xlat16_53 = (-u_xlat16_48);

    u_xlat40 = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.z;
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat40 * 3.14159274;
    u_xlat33.x = float(2);
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat40 * u_xlat33.x;
    u_xlat33.xy = (-u_xlat7.xy);
    u_xlat31.xy = u_xlat31.xy + u_xlat33.xy;
    u_xlat34 = sin(u_xlat40);
    u_xlat10.xw = cos(vec2(u_xlat40));
    u_xlat10.y = (-u_xlat34);
    u_xlat10.xw = u_xlat10.xw;
    u_xlat10.z = u_xlat34;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * vec4(0.5, 0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 + vec4(0.5, 0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat11 = vec4(ivec4(2, 2, 2, 2));
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat11;
    u_xlat11 = vec4(ivec4(1, 1, 1, 1));
    u_xlat11 = (-u_xlat11);
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 + u_xlat11;
    u_xlat33.x = dot(u_xlat31.xy, u_xlat10.xz);
    u_xlat33.y = dot(u_xlat31.xy, u_xlat10.yw);
    u_xlat7.xy = u_xlat7.xy + u_xlat33.xy;
    u_xlat7.xy = u_xlat7.xy;
    u_xlat31.xy = _MixMapUVDataLayerG.xy;
    u_xlat7.xy = u_xlat31.xy * u_xlat7.xy;
    u_xlat31.xy = _MixMapUVDataLayerG.zw;
    u_xlat7.xy = u_xlat31.xy + u_xlat7.xy;
    u_xlat32.xy = u_xlat9.xy + u_xlat7.xy;
    u_xlat8.xy = u_xlat8.xy;
    u_xlat8.zw = u_xlat32.xy;
    u_xlat7.xy = _MainTex_ST.xy;
    u_xlat7.xy = u_xlat7.xy * in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    u_xlat31.xy = _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat31.xy + u_xlat7.xy;
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat3.zw = u_xlat27.xy;
    u_xlat7.xyz = _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz + u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21.x = float(0.0);
    u_xlat16_21.y = float(0.0);
    u_xlat16_21.z = float(0.0);
    u_xlat16_21.xyz = u_xlat16_21.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21.xyz = u_xlat16_21.xyz;
    u_xlat9.x = 0.0;
    u_xlat16_9.x = u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat16_9.x = u_xlat16_9.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.w = u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_7.w = float(1);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.x = u_xlat16_9.x;
    u_xlat16_9.yzw = u_xlat16_21.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat2.xxxx * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0];
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat2.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 + u_xlat11;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat2.zzzz * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2];
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 + u_xlat11;
    u_xlat11 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3] * vec4(1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 + u_xlat11;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.x = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_7.xyz);
    u_xlat16_6.y = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_7.xyz);
    u_xlat16_6.z = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_7.xyz);
    u_xlat16_6.w = float(0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0 = u_xlat3;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat16_4;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_7;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = u_xlat16_9;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat10;
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = u_xlat16_0;
    vs_TEXCOORD9 = u_xlat8;
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = u_xlat16_6;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    return;
}

    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz / abs(u_xlat3.zzz);

    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat10;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 100.0;

    u_xlat1.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[0].z;
    u_xlat1.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[1].z;
    u_xlat1.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[2].z;
    u_xlat1.w = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[3].z;
    u_xlat0.w = 1.0;
    gl_Position.z = dot(u_xlat1, u_xlat0);
    u_xlat1.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[0].x;
    u_xlat1.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[2].x;
    u_xlat1.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[3].x;

    u_xlat1.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[2].y;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DigiBaseColor1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DigiHighColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _DigiScale;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_COLOR0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
float u_xlat4;
bool u_xlatb4;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat12;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).y;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = 0.0;
    u_xlat4 = u_xlat0.x * in_TEXCOORD0.y + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = min(u_xlat16_1.xx, vec2(1.0, 0.0));
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb4 = !!(u_xlat4>=u_xlat16_1.y);
#else
    u_xlatb4 = u_xlat4>=u_xlat16_1.y;
#endif
    u_xlat4 = u_xlatb4 ? 1.0 : float(0.0);
    u_xlat8 = (-u_xlat4) * u_xlat0.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat4;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_1.y * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-u_xlat16_1.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.xyw = u_xlat0.xxx * in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.w = u_xlat8;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(0.0500000007, 0.0500000007, 0.0500000007);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * vec3(_DigiScale) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyw * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat12 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat12 = max(u_xlat12, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat12 = inversesqrt(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.w = min(max(u_xlat1.w, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.w = clamp(u_xlat1.w, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_COLOR0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat12 = in_TEXCOORD0.y * 2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat1.z = (-_DigiChange) * 2.0 + u_xlat12;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.z = min(max(u_xlat1.z, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.z = clamp(u_xlat1.z, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xyw = in_TEXCOORD0.xyy;
    vs_TEXCOORD2 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 300 es

precision highp float;
precision highp int;
#define HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS 1
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
#define UNITY_UNIFORM
#else
#define UNITY_UNIFORM uniform
#endif
#define UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION 1
#if UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x) layout(location = x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(binding = x, std140)
#else
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(std140)
#endif
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _OutlineColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _OutlineWidth;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Offset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _lightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _ScreenResolution;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _DigiST1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DigiChange;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DigiBaseColor0;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DigiBaseColor1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DigiHighColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _DigiScale;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
float u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_3;
bool u_xlatb9;
mediump float u_xlat16_10;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0 = vs_TEXCOORD1.w * vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _DigiChange;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2 = (-_DigiBaseColor0) + _DigiBaseColor1;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_1.xxxx * u_xlat16_2 + _DigiBaseColor0;
    u_xlat16_3.xy = texture(_ClothTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xy;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb9 = !!(u_xlat16_1.w>=u_xlat16_3.x);
#else
    u_xlatb9 = u_xlat16_1.w>=u_xlat16_3.x;
#endif
    u_xlat16_10 = (u_xlatb9) ? u_xlat0 : 0.0;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_10;
    u_xlat16_2.x = _DigiChange + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_2.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * _DigiHighColor.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_10) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif
"
}
